<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ра́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мир-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-ниj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***замирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замирать.html>замира́ть</a> (5560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замирать.html>замира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замереть.html>замере́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand motionless, to freeze</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to a standstill</li>
<li>to die down (of a sound)</li>
<li>to sink (of the heart)</li>
<li>to falter (of the voice)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:замереть.html>замере́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a> (18012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мкнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to close</li>
<li>to surround</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">electricity</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to create a closed circuit, to short-circuit</li>
<li>to lock</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуться.html>замкну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamknútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкаться.html>замыка́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lock, to be locked</li>
<li>to be closed, to close <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круг.html>круг</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуться.html>замкну́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krug <b>zamknúlsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the circle closed up; it all came back to where it had started</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become/be sullen/withdrawn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуться.html>замкну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуться.html>замкну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорлупа.html>скорлупу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamknútʹsja</b> v sebé; <b>zamknútʹsja</b> v svojú skorlupú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to withdraw/retreat into oneself; go into one's shell</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***замминистра.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замминистра.html>замминистра</a> (17056)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Acronym of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заместитель.html>замести́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:министр.html>мини́стра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamestítelʹ minístra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замминистра.html>заммини́стра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamminístra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>deputy minister; vice-minister, undersecretary</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>за̀м<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ми.html>ми</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ни́с<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тра</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> согласовываться <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>частя́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>), несклоняемое (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 0  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***замок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замок</a> (1143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">zamek</i>, which is a calque via Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">zámek</i> of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">sloz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lock, keep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which, in turn, is a calque of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clūsa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lock, fort, fortification</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Attested from the 17th century. Related to <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamykatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).  But note also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Novgorod_dialect" class="extiw" title="w:Old Novgorod dialect">Old Novgorodian</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="zle-ono">ꙁамъке</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zle-ono-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamŭke</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lock</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zámok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>castle</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zamъkъ</i>, deverbal from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zamъknǫti</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamknútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>за́мок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zámok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Polish.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замко́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замочный.html>замо́чный</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замочка.html>замо́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lock <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fastener that opens with a key, or part of a firearm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американский.html>америка́нский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">amerikánskij <b>zamók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">springlock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">anglíjskij <b>zamók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">patent lock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">фити́льный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">fitílʹnyj <b>zamók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">matchlock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запирать.html>запира́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ворот.html>воро́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замо́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapirátʹ voróta na <b>zamók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lock the gate</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замке́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>zamké</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">under lock and key</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замок.html>замко́м</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pod <b>zamkóm</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">under lock and key</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> keystone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">jewelry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clasp, fastener</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замолкать.html>замолка́ть</a> (12287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолкнуть.html>замо́лкнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamólknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолкать.html>замолка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamolkátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолчать.html>замолча́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолкнуть.html>замо́лкнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become / fall silent, to stop / cease (speaking / talking), to break off</li></ol>

***замолчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замолчать.html>замолча́ть</a> (1934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">molčátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолчать.html>замолча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamolčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолкать.html>замолка́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become / fall silent, to stop / cease (speaking / talking), to break off</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замолчать.html>замолча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamolčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зама́лчивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to conceal, to keep secret, to cover up, to slur over, to veil, to hush up, to suppress</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заморозить.html>заморо́зить</a> (12947)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́з</a> (freeze, frost)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозить.html>заморо́зить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamorózitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замора́живать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">моро́зить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to freeze, to frost, to ice, to congeal</li></ol>
